Visibility from road great--Overall notes/how to bird:-This region looks awesome. There is no individual mother of all ranches/traps, but a series of ranches on the N side of the region (vicinity of 11th st) look very good. The best strategy is probably to focus on this region on the N end of the Valley. In Fall it would likely take about 4-5 hours to cover these spots well, in spring perhaps just 2-3.
